 vadodara or mehsana main do guton ke bich jamkar hangaamaa hua
 a fierce uproar ensued between two groups who came to vote in Hasanpur village of Visnagar in Mehsana district after which the militants ransacked
 donon ore se hue patharbaji main aadha darjan se zyada log jakhmi hue hai
 Bikes and vehicles parked nearby were burnt
 doosraa maamla vadodara jile kii sawali tehsil ke vaankaner gaanv main bhi to guton ke bich jamkar bavaal hua he
 Angry mob has set a motorcycle on fire
 police or paramilitary force ne tabadatodmaike par pahunchakar sthiti ko saamaanya karne ke liye uchit kadam uthaae
 Due to the stir, the voting process was interrupted and halted for half an hour
 bataa den ki police ke sakht kaarywai karke vaankaner gaanv main chust bandobast kar liya he
 Even during the second phase of the Gujarat election voting, the Congress has approached the Election Commission raising the issue of tampering with evms
 rajya ke mehsana main ek booth par iviem ke bluetooth se conect hone kaa aarope congress ne lagaaya he
 Deputy CM Nitin Patel is the BJP candidate from Mehsana Assembly seat and is pitted against Jeevabhai Patel of Congress
 is seat par donon partiyon ke bich kaante kaa muqabla najar aa rahaa he
 The Congress has accused a booth of Mehsana of connecting evms to Bluetooth
 congress ne kaha ki mehsana ke ekh booth par mobile phone kaa bluetooth on karne par ‘isio 105’ naam kaa ek upkaran uplabdh dikhaai detaa he
 This shows that EVM is being done through blue tooth
 gauratlab he ki pehle charan kii voting ke dauraan bhi congress kii ore se uske netaa arjuna morwadhia ne daawa kiya tha ki porbandar ke muslim bahul ilaake memnawada ketin matdaan kendron main electronic voting mashine bluetoothke jariye bahari upkarnon se judi hui hai
 Whenever a mobile phone's Bluetooth is turned on, a device called 'ECO 105' appears
 iskaa saaf matlab he ki bluetooth ke jariye upkaran kaa istemaal kar electronic voting mashiinon se chhedchhad kii ja sakati he
 Chief Electoral Officer (CEO) Bibi Swain, however, dismissed the Congress complaint saying that a polling agent had a mobile phone with 'ECO 105' inscribed as the model number
 isamen shikayatakarta ne isi ko chunaav ayog samaj liya
 In today's run-of-the-mill life, most people have become job professionals
 aise main 9-10 ghante offis main kaam kar ke thakne ke baad ghar jaakar khaanaa bananaa ek badi chunauti ho gai he
 In such a situation, eating outside seems to be a good option, but we all know how eating food outside every day spoils our budget
 isiilie jarurat he kuch aisi baton ko dhyaan main rakhane kii jisase aap baahar kaa khaanaa bhi kha sakate he or paise bhi bachaa sakate he
 Know these 10 tips: 1) Use coupons
 Whenever you go out to eat alone or with your family, try to use discount offers or coupons, it will not spoil your budget and you will also taste the taste of outside food
 Will be able to take
 2) tip dene se bachebgar aap kaa bajet kam he to koshish kare kii khaanaa khaane ke baad aap waiter ko tip na de
 By doing this you can save a little money while eating in the restaurant
 3) dinar ke bajaay lunch par jaaenye baat ham sab jaanate he ki dinar kii bajaay lunch sasta hota he
 That is why going to lunch instead of dinner is a good option to save money while eating outside
 4) drink lene se bacheksar ham dekhte he ki restaurant main koi bheedrink chaahe wo hard ho yaa soft mahangi milti he
 If you take this drink from an outside shop, then you can buy it for less money than in the restaurant, because the service charge is also added to the restaurant
 5) khaane ko baant kar khaaengar aap skool yaa college main padhate he yaa phir koi bhi jo baahar khaanaa kaa shaukin he to ye tarika aapkaa kaaphi paisa bachaayegaa
 Order anything and share it and eat it, you will be able to eat many varieties as well as you will have to pay less
 6) bane pasandida customerkai aise restaurant, dhabas yaa stall hote hai jo apane pasandida graahak ko special ophers dete he
 To do this you can like their website, Facebook page
 7) roj deal site check karengar aap baahar kaa khaanaa kam paise main khaanaa chaahate hai to kai cites he jis par har roj alag-alag aphers die jate he
 It is better that you stay constantly updated and enjoy delicious food for less money
 8) khaane ke baad meetha order karne se bachenzyaadaatar log khaanaa khaane ke baad swit dis order karte he jo ki unke bill ko badha detaa he
 Try not to order it and if you want to eat then buy from outside or pack it
 9) pani zyada pinaa chahiezyada se zyada pani pinaa sehat ke liye to phydemand he hi saath hi pani se pet bharaa rahata he to bhukh bhi kam lagati he
 In this case, outside orders are also reduced and money is saved
 10) bhukh ke hisaab se hi order karenkai baar aisa hota he ki ham kai cheez order kar dete hai or baad menkhaana zyada manga lene ke kaaran wo batch jaataa haior use phenkna padataa he
 That is why, order carefully
 bihar main bijepi ne kii enarasi taiyaar karne kii maangargedy ne kaha- simanchal main koi bhi bangladeshi nahisam ke tarj par ab bihar main bhi enarasi taiyaar karne kii maang uthne lagi he
 There has now been a demand from the BJP that NRC should be prepared in Bihar in the same manner as NRC has been prepared in Assam
 party netaa prem ranjan patel ne kaha ki rajya ke simanchal kshetra main jansankhya kaa santulan bighad gaya he jo kaaphi chintajanak he
 Prem Ranjan Patel said that Seemanchal region includes Purnia, Katihar, Araria and Kishanganj
 vahaan par jansankhya kaa santulan bighad gaya he or bangladeshi baari sankhya main vahaan par jameen rojgaar or vyapaar par kabiz hai
 He demanded that NRC list should also be prepared in Bihar so that those who are intruders can be excluded
 haalanki, bihar sarkaar main bijepi kii sahyogi jadyu ne pradesh main enarasi taiyaar karne kii maang ko puri tareeke se khaarij kar diya he
 Party spokesperson Rajiv Ranjan said that originally the Supreme Court had asked only to prepare NRC in Assam
 rajeev ranjan ne kaha ki assam main bhi jo enarasi taiyaar kiya gaya he, usamen kaaphi trutiyaan hai
 Because of which questions are being raised on its credibility
 is mudde par argedy bhi jediu ke saath khadi dikh rahi he
 The RJD said that the BJP government is buoying the NRC issue to divert attention from the serious issue of recession and declining growth in the country
 party vidhayak abu dujana ne kaha ki bijepi vidhansabha chunaav se pehle bihar main dharmik dhruvikaran karnaa chaahati he
 The RJD rejected that anyone in Seamanchal lives in Bangladesh
 dilli main 15 agast se pehle hathiyaaron kaa ek bada jakhira pakadaa gaya he

 com / wdklyworar— ICC (@icc)april 23, 2015 The NDA government in Bihar is currently working hard to strengthen its vote bank
 daliton main naaraazgi ko dekhte hue nitish sarkaar ne pehle sirf essi / asti ke upiessi or bipiessi kii praarambhik pariksha (piti pariksha) paas karne par protsaahan raashi dene kaa elaan kiya tha
 But now the government has decided to include candidates from backward and very backward classes as well
 iske tahat soobe menessi / astiki tarah pichhadaa or ati pichhadaa varg ke abhyarthiyon ko upiessi kii piti paas karne par ek lakh rupee or bipiessi kii piti pariksha paas karne par 50 hajaar rupee kii protsaahan raashi rajya sarkaar degi
 Now only general category candidates will be deprived of this incentive amount of Nitish government
 pichde varg ke abhyarthiyon ne sarkaar ke is kadam kaa swaagat kiya he
 Students preparing for these competitive examinations in Patna said that this is a very commendable step by the nitishsarkar
 bipiessi kii taiyaari kar rahe vishaal kumaar, ashish ranjan, rabindra kumaar or shravan kumaar kaa kahana he ki sarkaar ko piti pariksha ke turant baad yah raashi chaatro ko uplabdh karnaa chahie, taaki wo samay par koching kar saken
 They say that many students from backward and extremely backward classes are not able to prepare for Mains properly after passing PT due to lack of money
 pichley hafte rajya cabinet ne sabase pehle essi / asti ke chaatro ke liye protsaahan raashi dene kaa faisla kiya tha
 It was then being said that Dalits are angry and to make them happy, the government has taken this decision
 iske thik ek hafte baad sarkaar ko yahi faisla pichhadaa or ati pichhada varg ke liye bhi lenaa padaa
 Prem Singh Meena, Secretary, Backward and Extremely Backward Classes Welfare Department of the government, says that due to lack of money, students of these sections were not able to properly prepare for competitive examinations
 wo behatar koching nahin le pate the
 Now with the money received from the state government, they can do excellent preparation by coaching
 is faisle par chaatro ne khush jaahir kii he, lekin unhen dar he ki sarkaar kaa yah faisla sirf kaagaj par hi na rah jaae
 They also demand that they get money on time so that they can take coaching on time
 haalanki sarkaar ke is faisle se aarthik rup se pichde saamaanya varg ke chaatro kii bhi aas jaagi he ki shaayad sarkaar unki bhi sud le
 Aam Aadmi Party's national member Preeti Menon has accused former BJP minister Eknath Khadse of duping the government for a thousand crore rupees
 priti menon ne pune main ek patrkaar vaarta ko sambodhit karte hue ekanath khadse par aarope lagaaya ki pune ke namchin builder avinaash bhonsle ko pachaas karod kaa phayda karaane ke chakkar main unhone rajya sarkaar ko ek hajaar karod bataur property najarana maaf kar dene vaala order diya
 Preeti Menon told that in Vijay Nagar area of pune, the government had kept about 24 acres of land for the gazetted officer
 ye plot pune ke shivajinagar ke i squaire multiplex ke paas he
 Preeti Menon said, 'this issue is a big property issue of Pune, which was put up by the government for the gazetted officers
 vijay nagar ke 200 plots gagetted officers ko die jaaenge, wo plots lij par die jaaenge
 Those plots cannot be sold further
 agar bechnaa he, to mul maalikon ko sarkaar se ijaajat leni hongi or unhen sarkaar ko 50 fisadi cell vailu deni hongi
 'an NGO committed the scandal,' Fodpriti Menon said that more than 90 per cent of the plots have been sold in this property and the government has not accepted their sight

 Nearly four years after the 10 Pakistani terrorists were killed in Mumbai, India on Saturday launched its surveillance radar network to guard the beaches of Maharashtra and Gujarat
 yah network suraksha main us chook kii bharpai karegaa jis kaaran mumbai main 26 / 11 ke hamale hue the
 Defense Minister AK Antony inaugurated the coastal monitoring system (static sensor chain) in Mumbai and Porbandar, taking a major step towards strengthening the security apparatus of the country's coastlines spread over 7,500 km
 unhone bharosa diya ki 2013 ke madhya tak desh ke sabhi samudri taton, mukhyabhumi or dwipon donon par lagaataar tateey chaukasee pariyojna puri kar lee jaaegi
 It is the first coastal surveillance network with stationary radars and electrically operated sensors at 84 remote sites, including the insular area bordering the coast
 yah network samudr main chalate hue sandigdh jahaajon va naukaaon kii pahchaan karne main madadgaar sabit hoga
 After the inauguration, Antony said monitoring the Indian coastal region is a challenging task
 tateey nigaraanee network kii sthapana se tat rakshakon kii electronic chaukasee kshamta badhegi
 Antony also said that the western coastal region of the country is extremely sensitive
 isliye maharashtra or gujarat main is network kii sthapana sabase pehle karne kaa faisla liya gaya
 The sensors in this network will be operated from radar stations
 ye radar stesan tarapur, korlai, tolakeshwar or devgad main tatarakshak sthir samvedak pariyojna ke hisse ke rup main sthapit kiye gaye hai
 The comments yah network tateey suraksha tantra kaa ek mahatvapurn ghatak he jo samudri yatayaat kii pahchaan or nigaraanee sunishchit karegaa
 He informed that in the first phase of this project, the network will be expanded to 46 sites and care will be taken that it can be monitored up to 25 nautical miles at the right time
 mumbai or porbandar main chaukasee radar network ke udghaatan avasar par raksha utpaadan sachiv shekhar agarwal, bhartiya tatraksha mahanideshak vaais admiral em
